 baharhaal, madhya railway kii harbar or madhya line par sthaneey train aaj subah deree se chal rahi he

 yatriyon ko koi badi asuvidha nahin hui

 offis main kaam ke dauraan aksar ham khud ko thakaa hua mahasoos karte hai
 Sometimes this fatigue is due to work pressure and sometimes due to tension filled environment of office
 aise main offis routine ke dauraan aajamaayen ye tips or mast hokar karen offis ke kaam:1
 Let Personal Problem Be Personal: It is often seen that we sit down to solve our personal problem in the office
 is tarah ham apane offis time ko kharaab karte hai or personal life main bhi pareshaaniyaan badha lete hai
 So always remove your personal problem from your mind and only enter it in the office
 2
 Build your corner in the office: We spend the longest time in our office 24 hours a day
 aise main jaruri he ki vahaan par hamaari jarurat kii sabhi chijen maujuud hon
 Manage your seating area by following office rules
 is tarah aap kaam ke saath comfort bhi mahasoos kar sakenge
 3
 problem ko karen share:kaam ke dauraan agar aap ko kisi cheez se koi dikkat he to use apane saath kaam karne waalon ko jarur bataaen
 Many times, we do not tell our problems to the people around us and take useless pressure
 yahi nahin kisi project ko lekar aapaki kya soch he is baat ko bhi khul kar rakhen
 4
 khan-paan kaa rakhen khyaal:offis ke dauraan sabase ahm cheez hoti he hamaari diet, jise ham kaam ke chalate aksar najrandaaj kar baithte hai
 Never forget to eat and drink during work as it is possible to work only when you are healthy
 5
 Learn to manage work: The right management plays the best role in making your work easy and productive
 isliye time rahete hue kaam ko puraa karnaa or sahi tareeke se karne kii aadat daalen
 6
 khud ko den reword:jab kabhi aap apane target ko puraa karen to khud ko reword dena nahin bhoolen
 By doing this, your confidence increases and you feel fresh in yourself
 7
 Don't forget to take a break: By taking a break, you are able to work better
 bek lenaa isliye bhi jaruri he kyonki ye kaam se aapke andar ai thakaan ko mitaane kaa sabase acha tarika he
 8: Keep positive thinking: Positive thinking is effective to boost your life
 aise main kisi ghatana se apane andar nakaaratmak soch laane se pehle uske sabhi pahaluon par acchhee tarah soch-vichaar jarur kar len
 In the 54th Council meeting of NCERT, Delhi Government Education Minister Manish Sisodia presented a review report on the books
 is report main sisodiya ne kitabon ke chepter, prigentation or bhashaa par aapatti jataai he
 Union Minister Prakash Javadekar and education officers of several states should also be present in the council meeting

 bjp's prime ministerial candidate Narendra Modi won the Vadodara seat by 5,70,128 votes
 jila colector evam nirvachan adhikari vinod raav ne kaha, hamane bijepi ke narendra modi ko vadodara sansadeey seat se vijeta ghoshit kiya he
 Modi got 11 in total
 63 lakh voton main se 8,45,464 vot mili
 His nearest rival Congress general secretary Madhusudan Mistry received 2,75,336 votes, while the bail of six other candidates including Aam Aadmi Party's Sunil Kulkarni will be forfeited in the election fray
 aisa isliye, kyonki ve nunatam mat praapt karne main asafal rahe

 2009 ke chunaav main bijepi ke baaluu shukla yahaan se 1
 It was won by 36 lakh votes
 bijepi ke ek sthaneey netaa ne kaha, vadodara seat par yah sabase adhik antar se jeet he or ham ummid karte hai ki 2014 ke is chunaav main yah desh bhar main sabhi siton main sabase adhik antar vaali jeet hogi
 State Bank of India (SBI) has now announced to abolish the IMPS charge from 1 August 2019
 darasal bhartiya rigerv bank (RBI) ke aadesh ke baad desh ke sabase bade bank bhartiya state bank ne 1 july se enift or artijies par lagane vaale charge hataa die hai
 The transaction charges are being abolished by the RBI for the purpose of promoting digital transactions
 isi kadi main ab bank ne iempies (tatkaal bhugtan seva) se lenden karne par bhi ek agast se shulk hataane kaa nirnay kiya he
 It is worth noting that RTGS is used for large amount of transactions and NEFT system for transactions up to two lakh rupees
 bank kaa kahana he ki yono, internet banking or mobile banking ke madhyam se fund transfar karne vaale yugers se ab kisi tarah kaa iempies charge nahin vasula jayega
 This is a big relief for SBI customers
 ab iempies lenden par bhi koi shulk nahin dena padegaa
 YONO (you Only Need One) is the name of an app that brings together the bank's digital and lifestyle platforms
 iske panjikrut graahakon kii sankhya kareeb ek karod he
 SBI has 6 crore internet banking customers, while 1
 41 karod log mobile banking kaa istemaal karte hai
 The bank's digital platform YONO is used by 10 million customers
 kya hota he iempimediat pement sarvice (iempies) ke instent interbank electronic fund transfar sarvice he, jo mobile phone or atm jaise anya channels, internet banking ke madhyam se kii jaati he
 In the case of IMPS, the funds reach the beneficiary's account immediately
 yon utpeedan ke maamle main fanse asaram kii mushkilen kam hone kaa naam nahin le rahi hai
 Now investigation will start against Asaram in Jammu too
 ye maamla jammu sthit ashram main teen bacchon ko kathith rup se dafnaae jane kaa he
 The court has directed the police to investigate afresh
 jald hi jammu police asaram se poochtacha kar sakati he
 a man named Bholanandar, who was close to Asaram, claimed that the bodies were buried in the premises of the ashram after the mysterious death of the three children
 is khulaase ke baad ek enjio ne adaalat main maamle kii jaanch kii guhaar lagaai thi
 Bholananda claimed that he had worked in Asaram's Jammu ashram for nearly seven years
 is dauraan jammu ke ashram main teen bacchon kii rahasyamay paristhitiyon main maut ho gayi thi jiske baad un teenon bacchon ko ashram parisar main hi dafnaaya gaya tha
 Not only this, Bholananda had also claimed that if he was taken to the ashram of Jammu under police protection, he would also identify the place where these children were buried
 bholanand ke is khulaase ke baad jammu kii ek gaiyr sarkari sanstha ol india kisaan seva sangh kii taraf se adaalat main guhaar lagaayi gai ki is maamle kii jaanch kii jaae
 The court, after hearing the case, has directed the Jammu police to investigate the matter thoroughly
 adaalat ne police ko maamle kii chaanbin kar adaalat ko report dene ko kaha he
 Jammu Police has said that it will soon inquire into this matter and if need be, a case will also be registered soon
 25 oktober tak jail main rahenge asaramudhar, gujarat police shanivaar ko asaram ko ahmedabad le ja sakati he
 On Friday, the Jodhpur court ordered transit remand to the Gujarat Police
 vahi jodhpur seshan court ne asaram kii nyaayik hiraasat badha di
 Now he will have to remain in jail till 25 October
 shilpi, shiva, sharatchand or prakaash kii nyaayik hiraasat bhi 25 oktober tak badha di gai he

 Lok Sabha Speaker Sumitra Mahajan has arranged that Godse is no longer a non-parliamentary term except for mention about Nathuram Ram Godse
 sansad ne 1956 main is shabd ke istemaal par pratibandh laga diya tha
 Mahatma Gandhi was assassinated by Nathuram Godse in 1948 in New Delhi
 pratibandh hataane kaa aadesh guuruuvaar ko paarit hua
 This has brought considerable relief to Shiv Sena MP from Nashik, Hemant Tukaram Godseco, who sought to remove the word Godse from the list of non-parliamentary words
 hemanth tukaraam godse ne donon sadanon ke peethasin adhikariyon ko likhe patron main is baat par aashcharya jataayaa tha ki kisi saansad ke upnaam ko asansadeey kaise mana ja saktaa he
 He insisted on removing the word from the list of unparliamentary words, it is certainly not my fault that my surname is Godse and apart from that i cannot and will not change it as it is my paternal surname
 unhone daleel di thi ki pratibandh mere upnaam or mere purvajon par anuchit kalank lagaataa he
 He said that there are a large number of people of Godse community who live in different parts of Maharashtra and that too belongs to this community
 shivasena saansad ne swayan ko tab ajeeb sthiti main paaya jab rajyasabha ke up sabhapati ne sheetakaaleen satr ke dauraan ek sadsy ko godse shabd istemaal karne se roak diya tha kyonki vah asansadeey tha
 The member came to know that Parliament had decided to ban the word Godseper in 1956, after which the Speaker passed the order, now the name Godse will not be called unparliamentary as a surname
 keval nathuram godse kaa ullekh asansadeey hoga
 The list will be changed accordingly
 -input bhashaa Notification has been issued for the seventh and final phase of Uttar Pradesh Assembly elections
 is charan main pradesh ke saat jilon kii 40 vidhansabha siton par chunaav honge
 According to the Election Commission, notification was issued at 11 am for the seventh and final phase of the state assembly elections
 iske saath hi is charan ke liye namakan prakriya bhi shuru ho gai
 Nominations will be filed by 16 February, which will be examined on 17 February
 namakan waapas lene kii antim tithi 20 farvari hogi, jabaki matdaan aath march ko hoga
 In the seventh and final phase, elections will be held for 40 assembly seats in Ghazipur, Varanasi, Jaunpur, Chandauli, Mirzapur, Bhadohi and Sonbhadra districts
 is charan main ek karod 41 lakh 39 hajaar 697 matadaata apane matadhikaron kaa prayog kar sakenge, jisamen lagbhag lagbhag 76
 62 lakh men and about 64
 76 lakh mahila matadaata evam 707 anya shrenee ke matadaata shaamil hai
 8,682 polling stations and 14,458 polling places have been set up for this phase of polling
 tippaniyan Even in the seventh phase in the 2012 assembly elections, the SP won 23 out of 40 seats in a strong performance
 iske alaava basapa ko paanch, bhaajapa ko chaar or congress ko teen siten mili thim
